ANEXO
anexo Decisión BCE modificará
artículo sustituirán definiciones siguientes
payer except where used in Article means TARGET participant whose PM account will be debited as result of payment order being settled
artículo apartado letra sustituirá
in the ECB’s assessment such participation would endanger the overall stability soundness and safety of TARGETECB or of any other TARGET component system would jeopardise the ECB’s performance of its tasks as described in the Statute of the European System of Central Banks and of the European Central Bank or poses risks on the grounds of prudence
artículo apartado letras sustituirán siguientes
the ECB suspends limits or terminates the participant’s access to intraday credit pursuant to paragraph of Annex III to Guideline ECB
artículo modificará
título Data protection prevention of money laundering and related issues sustituido Data protection prevention of money laundering administrative or restrictive measures and related issues
añadirá apartado
Participants when acting as the payment service provider of payer or payee shall comply with all requirements resulting from administrative or restrictive measures imposed pursuant to Articles or of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union including with respect to notification and or obtaining consent from competent authority in relation to the processing of transactions
For the purposes of this paragraph the terms payment service provider payer and payee shall have the meanings given to them in the applicable administrative or restrictive measures
payee except where used in Article means TARGET participant whose PM account will be credited as result of payment order being settled
when the ECB is the payment service provider of participant that is payer
the participant shall make the required notification or obtain consent on behalf of the central bank that is primarily required to make notification or obtain consent and shall provide the ECB with evidence of having made notification or having received consent and
the participant shall not enter any credit transfer order into TARGET until it has obtained confirmation from the ECB that the required notification has been made or the consent has been obtained by or on behalf of the payment service provider of the payee
when the ECB is payment service provider of participant that is payee the participant shall make the required notification or obtain consent on behalf of the central bank that is primarily required to make notification or obtain consent and shall provide the ECB with evidence of having made notification or having received consent
